## Surprising Connections (you probably didn't know these)
- `formatDuration()` --calls--> `floor()`  [INFERRED]
  n8n-master/scripts/build-n8n.mjs → src/lib/sabflow/n8n/extensions/number-extensions.ts
- `getNodeParameter()` --calls--> `configureActivityCallback()`  [INFERRED]
  src/lib/sabflow/n8n/core/execution-engine/node-execution-context/node-execution-context.ts → n8n-master/packages/@n8n/nodes-langchain/nodes/vendors/Microsoft/microsoft-utils.ts
- `getNodeParameter()` --calls--> `getParameter()`  [INFERRED]
